et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations; et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption: par aventure feroit venir la mort.	And never does the swelling appear behind the shoulder blade, and take care that this is not a dislocation; for this is the bone that breaks, for which we must not have any presumption: for in this case death may come by chance.
des dislocations de la hainche	Dislocations of the shoulder
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures; et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc .iiij. parties: dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier; et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	Dislocations of the shoulder are only caused by dislocations of the shoulder and elbow joints; they do not occur with other joints. The dislocation of the shoulder is impaired in three parts: front and back, and above and below; the greater the displacement in front and back, the greater the impairment.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of dislocation is that when the limb is joined with the limb, if it is longer and the patient’s knee is wider than the normal, and the patient cannot double his knee at the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and this is the bruise that is left behind the cautery, for in this way the head of the femur comes to rest.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of the one who comes to the rescue, if it is that this accident is contrary to those mentioned above.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement; toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	And the sign of the one who comes to the rescue, if it is that his limb is well according to completion; however, do not double the knee joint in pain, and if you see him forced to do so, if he cannot do so before, and retains his urine, and swells the ankle, and when he walks, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the sign of the one who comes to the rescue, if it is that he cannot extend his knee, cannot double it, and that this limb is shorter than the other, and the ankle is softened, and the shoulder is dislocated at the root of the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure; et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	The repeated displacement of this semblance of dislocation must be treated, for if it is an ancient dislocation and remains as before, it endures according to its setting; and there is no cure; and I do not know that there is any presumption.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des .iiij. manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre; par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	If the dislocation is recent and there are three ways of dislocation, if you are hasty and turn the joint, stretch it inwards and outwards, and move it to the right and left; by chance, if it returns, there is no need for any other cure.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles .i. ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a .ij. mains, ou a .i. liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this way, if you must take four strong assistants, and stretch the limb strongly with two hands, or with one hand as you please;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe; et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And another minister extends his hand downwards as far as his elbows, then grasps it with a strip of linen over the hip; and another holds the head of the linen.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And extend upwards and downwards all at once, until the patient is lifted from the ground at once, and rests suspended.</start_of_turn>
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as .iiij. semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is often used as in three similar cases, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is well.</start_of_turn>
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance. de la dislocation dou genoil	of dislocation of the shoulder
Li genous est desaluez selonc .iij. manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee is evacuated according to two methods: that is to say, inwards and outwards, and backwards; and do not evacuate it forward.

de la dislocation dou talon	of dislocation.
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The talons never is esteemed, neither fully dislocated, but always partially.

et fai ce .ij. fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	et fai ce trois fois, si com nos avons dit, en monast et en traçant le pied; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient.

Then place the eyes evenly over the dislocation at their hands, and another assistant grasps the limb firmly at the shoulder, and the dislocation will return immediately.</start_of_turn>

des dois	then.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the bones are dislocated, if you can extend the limb well, it is a light thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus .i. leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is not in any knot of the back or the shoulder, then you must make the patient sit upright on a chair or table, and place your hand on what is open of these joints, then press your hand firmly until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a .ij. chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse .iij. jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when it is equal, and nothing is open, if you place a stool under the limb at the shoulder, then press firmly, and leave it for two days, then take it off; and rest it until it is healed.</start_of_turn>
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	This excerpt describes various medical procedures, including cautery for hair removal, treatment of dislocations and bleeding, and setting of dislocated shoulders.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and it is seen to be restored, many times it has happened that the patient died.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you do not show humility in the cure, and if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not merciful, compassionate, and timely, do not attempt it;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and use soothing things at the beginning, such as cautery, and leave the patient in the hand of God, if you do not see hope of health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, if you now reset the limb, even though the swelling remains;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is at rest, if necessary, administer calming things about the wound, and cure the wound, if possible, with dried oils.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is a fracture with a dislocation, and soft bones break, if the bones fracture, do as has been said in simple illnesses;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors. Amen	And take care not to enter into fear, as I have said, for this will bring you harm according to your Creator, and for the salvation of your soul and body. Amen.
Explicit le romen de fisique	Praise be to physical medicine.
